Source: 新法律自 1 月 1 日起生效，要求警察只有在应对对警察或周围人员的致命威胁的“必要时刻”，才能使用致命武力。

Source: 新法律自 1 月 1 日起生效，要求警察只有在应对对警察或周围人员的致命威胁的“必要时刻”，才能使用致命武力。

Translation: The new law, which takes effect Jan. 1, will allows police to use deadly force only when"necessary" to defend against an imminent threat of death or serious injury to officers or bystanders.

Major errors:

1. "will allows" should be "will allow" (grammar agreement)
2. "necessary" should be "necessary to" (semantic addition)
3. "imminent threat of death or serious injury to officers or bystanders" should be "imminent threat of death or serious injury to officers or bystanders" (semantic omission)

Corrected translation:

The new law, which takes effect Jan. 1, allows police to use deadly force only when necessary to defend against an imminent threat of death or serious injury to officers or bystanders.

Note: The corrected translation maintains the original meaning of the source text, but with improved grammar and clarity.

1. "是" (shì) is a linking verb that indicates the subject's state or condition. In this sentence, "是" is used to indicate that the subject "这名男子" (zhè míng nán zǐ) is in a critical but stable condition.
2. "严重烧伤" (yán zhòng shāo jiāng) is a phrase that indicates the subject's physical state. It should be followed by a preposition "from" to indicate the cause of the subject's condition.
3. "在医院" (zài yī yuàn) is a prepositional phrase that indicates the location where the subject is. It should be followed by a comma.
4. "情况" (qíng kè) is a noun phrase that indicates the subject's condition. It should be followed by a comma.
5. "但" (dàn) is a conjunction that indicates a contrast or a contradiction. It should be followed by a comma.
